< Review>
I recently brought my boat to Santa Clarita Auto Sound, I have for years wanted to update and improve the sound system in it I just never knew how, and thought the amount of custom work would just be way to expensive for me to afford.  I contacted Santa Clarita Auto Sound, who was referred to me by my boat mechanic.  When I dropped the boat off,  I discussed my needs and was assured that they could take care of everything I wanted.  Let me Tell you that the end result was better than I imagined, and the craftsmanship of the custom parts was exquisite.  They answered all of my concerns and checked to make sure that I approved of any custom installation that was not originally discussed, they even were able to accommodate a quick connect amplifier system. As many boat owners know when we store our boats theft of such Audio systems is a big problem.  I would definitely recommend Santa Clarita Auto Sound to anyone.  I think that you will be more than pleased with their work.<//Review>

< text>
Being a touring musical technical professional, with a focus on guitar system configuration, I ended up cursed with an extensively trained and absurdly finicky ear. I was never satisfied with any system configuration or tuning that I had assembled or had installed in my vehicle(s). So when it came time to, again, attempt to satisfy my craving for flawless audio in my vehicle, I shuddered. Along came Henry at Santa Clarita Autosounds. I went in. I met Henry. I was jaded and apprehensive. I gave the short speech about what I do for a living, etc. and postured myself (rather arrogantly, actually) as an educated consumer, not to be swindled. I stated what I wanted and a budget. I was stunned at the response. I was greeted with something that I hadn't experienced before. Ears. This guy was actually LISTENING to me. I couldn't believe it. Henry was patient, professionally consultative (which I really related to and quite liked) and funny. No "close 'em" attitude at all. He went to work, exploring and explaining options that all fell within my stated preferences. I settled on a system and took a chance. Boy, am I glad I did. I (and my pesky ears) have never been more satisfied or happier with the result. Henry has never played any sort of games with me. And believe me, I would know. He is courteous, professional and put the stuff in (and tuned my vehicle's audio response - really cool) in a timely manner and pleasantly within budget. I highly recommend this business.< /text>

I waited a little while to calm down before writing this. Having said that, I still WOULD NOT RECOMMEND this place even it was the only one in town. But they gave me a 20% discount over the phone and could get me in the same day, so I went. I had the tint installed, but I had to bring it back the next weekend to have them replace some tint film that had been scratched during installation.

After getting my car back the second time, I went home and the car literally stayed parked in the garage for two days. On the third day I decided to wash the car, which is when I noticed hard impact paint damage under the front bumper that appeared to have been touched up by a shoddy paint job. I'm not talking about a few small scratches either. So I took the car back in to show them the damage. <Text>This place is a little gem. It's like the Chiptole of Asian flavor-based sushi bowls. Simple, clean and simply delicious. You kind of have to do a little thinking/choosing, but it's so worth it. The 3-step menu guide above steers you to making your own customized bowl of sushi yumminess. Each one is a unique masterpiece! (or you can order pre-decided flavor profiles so you dont have to think... but you want to think, don't you?!). When you do the right and brave thing to create your own bowl don't panic with all the choices before you. Breathe. Just pick what you like and be confident. You can do this.

I should have taken a pic of mine, but it looked so good I ate it before I could take a picture (that ever happen to you?). This is a little place that has a few inside tables so you can eat there if you like, or great for take out, which I usually do so I can rip into it without people witnessing my unfettered gluttony.

Some advice: they are so generous with their servings I can only finish a small size ($6.95 + tax) bowl so maybe start with that. Fantastic deal for the quality and portions. Healthy and tasty. Always friendly staff and clean location. Go catch you some Pinkfish Poke.< /Text>< userid>

<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
I bought the carry on and medium suitcases in white about six months ago. I made the purchase through the website, and everything went as smoothly as can be. Delivery came earlier than expected, and the suitcases were in perfect condition. I've used the carry on the most (since I travel mostly for work), and it's been much better than I'd hoped. It carries more than you'd think and the battery/charger is so convenient. Slowly, scuff marks had been building up, and it really took a beating on this last trip. So I pulled out a Mr. Clean Magic Eraser, as suggested, and started cleaning it. I was shocked at how quickly and how well the suitcase cleaned up. The attached pictures show the before and after of 5 minutes of cleaning (with one side of the case being the before and the other the after, both having very similar marks). There are still a few deeper, darker scuffs, but I think they'll come out with a more concentrated cleaning. Besides, it's white; I expected it to get a little banged up. It's amazing how little that has happened, though. Thoroughly recommend this luggage. It's fantastic and well worth the money.</Text>

< Text>
These five stars reflect both Away as a company and my experience at the LA store. When it was suggested to me to spend over $200 on a carry-on bag after I grew up with $50 discount store bags it seemed excessive. We decided to give it a try and went ahead and ordered the first generation carry-on not long after launch. We loved the bag so much that as soon as they released their large bag we went ahead and ordered the generation one large bag as well. Fast forward a few years and I am in need of an additional carry-on bag. I saw that Away started producing aluminum luggage and when I saw it came in a half the price of all the aluminum suitcases I avoided over the years I went ahead and made the purchase. It is absolutely stunning. While there I was speaking with the team members about our other two away bags and when I mentioned one was giving me trouble with the lock, they suggested I bring it in. They tried to fix it but were unable so they went ahead and replaced the bag for me under the lifetime warranty. If we weren't customers for life before we definitely are now. Finding honest customer service to stand by their product is rare today. Away hits the perfect spot where the price is still achievable for most people but the product and service are that of a much more expensive bag.<//Text>

< Review>
My wife's 1996, Z28 Camaro was making a loud, irregular, metallic, rattling, sound upon startup last week. This awful sound was coming from beneath the engine. Had to quickly turn off the ignition for fear of more damage. Spoke to Viet in the morning, and had it towed using a flatbed truck to Precise Auto Repair. Since my wife and I really like this car, we were hoping that it was not a broken rod; engine problem because that is what it sounded like. Viet called in the afternoon, and said he had some good news. The problem was that the starter motor's gear housing (next to the front roll drive) was cracked, and a piece of this metallic housing was hitting the flywheel gears as it rotated (yikes). Good news was that nothing was wrong with the motor! We felt like we dodged a bullet on that one!  Viet replaced the old starter with a brand new, Delco, starter which was slightly more expensive than a rebuilt one, but was worth it to me. Thank you, Viet. You are a keeper. Our experience prompted me to write this positive review. This was on Valentine's day, so it was especially fitting.< /Review>

< Review>
It's really hard to find a good mechanic so I was happy to stumble upon Precise.

My first experience was with Viet, who helped me service my van's broken a/c.  Within an hour, I drove out with air again.  I don't remember how much it cost ... Just that I was pleasantly surprised.  While Viet was very down to business, he was also friendly.

Since that time, I've interacted mostly with Tom.  Tom has taken good care of my cars.  He's great at explaining what the plan is, initially, and later, what they did.  If he replaces parts, he typically sets aside the old parts and if he can, he literally shows you why they were defective.  That's a level of detail that I rarely see.

I've had both small and big services since then.  Lately, they replaced my Subaru Outback engine with a rebuild.  Because of the boxer-type engine, the common suggestion is to take your Subaru to a Subaru specialist (either the dealer/mechanic or to a specialist mechanic).  Well, the only specialist I knew of in my area got pretty meh reviews online ... so I had Tom/Precise do it and now my car feels as good as, if not better than ever!

I walked in to their office the other day and overheard somebody saying that they've been with Precise for years and they've moved around the Bay.  And while he currently lives in the _San Francisco_, he and his partner still travel all the way down to Santa Clara/Sunnyvale to get their cars serviced at Precise.

Now, that's loyalty ... and I can totally understand why.< /Review>

< Review>
Great, honest place. I had gone to another place in southern california to get my O2 sensor changed, and the person tried to tell me my radiator was "leaking" and said it also needs to be replaced. I decided to come back to the bay area to get a second opinion. When I came here to get some other O2 sensor changed, I didn't tell them what the other folks said about my radiator, but these people also said the radiator is maybe leaking, but it is a small leak and they just refilled with coolant and told me to keep an eye on it. The price for the O2 sensor change was reasonable and they only charged 6 dollars to refill coolant. I came another time 8 months later to ask if my radiator was leaking and another technician came to look at it, and he also said it wasn't a problem. It's a super tiny leak, and I still had plenty of coolant. So, in summary, both technicians I met were really honest and not trying to get extra money off of changing my radiator (which would be like 800+ dollars), unlike the auto shop in Rowland heights (southern california). <Text>I can't say enough how terrific Scott and Richard is! I needed to get a small 5x5 storage unit that day. They are very understanding and listened to my situation.
We all know how google maps work when searching for a place. Though, don't let high reviews fool you, always visit them to see the location and talk with the staff in person.  Be kind and personable and you'll find out how they care about their work. Happy employees make for a happier business.  Anyhow.....

Upon researching online and visiting different Self Storage websites.... I've noticed there is a lot of online deals to be had right on their websites.  I narrowed it down to 4 different Self Storages. They all have very competitive prices online.  Though, one is way cheaper but does not compare to how well the other 3 maintain their properties.

Of the 4, I was able to narrow it down to just 2 Self Storages.  They both had great customer service, clean facilities, excellent security features and knew their business well.  Very close in rental prices online too.

Richard was helping me. Scott the manager, was helping another customer and I couldn't help but listen on the side. Great and awesome people!

Richard was able to answer all my questions and then some.  Security is top notch here.
- Gated with keypad
- Individually alarmed units
- Vented outside air into their facility. I couldn't find a climate controlled Self Storage around due to my time constraint and wanted to stay in carlsbad by Palomar Airport.
- They do use a special kind of lock that is set inside of the roll up doors with star keys. No hinges on their doors for padlocks. Another added security feature.  I don't mind.... I'll use StorQuest again in a heartbeat.
- Customer restroom. Well taken care of
- Surveillance system
- Free carts to use to move your goods
- Large Elevators
- Main building has a covered loading dock
- Well maintained
- Clean. Inside and out. Just a beautiful location
- Boxes and accessories if you need to buy.
- Go ask them about different leasing times.
- They do have different tiers on access times.  No 24 hour access.

- Though you have to buy storage rental insurance from them or provide your own.  An added cost, but I didn't mind for the price I was given.

Do check them out if you are looking! Check out their website first for availability and call if you have any questions about StorQuest. I feel very safe here and for my stuff.

I've added photos and a few videos of this place

P.S. All their doors are in the process of a color change.  Don't be alarmed if their outside doors are red and inside is blue. I went to 4 different places between Oceanside and Carlsbad where I came across either rude/unhelpful management of exorbitant prices. First off, this place is CLEAN! Other places just don‚Äôt come close to the attractiveness and cleanliness of this place. And second, and high up on the list: both the manager, Scott Jedlick and his assistant, Richard offer great customer service. Prior to getting this storage unit, I checked out several places (over the phone and in person). During this period (person and phone), I talked to both Scott and Richard and they explained things well and came across as very professional, plus the rate I was quoted was extremely competitive. I got a 10‚Äô X 15‚Äô unit with StorQuest that was less expensive that some other places‚Äô 10‚Äô X 10‚Äô units.

I was a little hesitant about a second story unit, but Richard pointed out the dollies around the facility and with being able to park right next to the elevator (and with my unit being close to the elevator), I found that my initial fears were unwarranted. It was easy to access my unit, and to move things in and out of it.

At this place, they have you purchase a cylinder lock (~ $20.00 plus tax) to lock your unit. This is a very secure type of lock! In the past, at another storage facility, I had my lock cut open and my unit broken into. When I told this to StorQuest manager, Scott, he explained how secure and virtually-tamper proof these cylinder locks are.

There was one more thing that I really liked about this place: after punching in your code at the entrance, the buildings are arranged so that you drive (in one direction) in a big square and exit at the other side (where you again punch in your code for the exit gate to open). This seemed safer to me than cars and trucks coming and going in different directions, and like I said before, I was able to park right next to the elevator in my building. The driving space/path between the buildings was quite adequate so that cars and trucks could easily pass around cars parked to the side.

I had my unit at StorQuest for about 6 months until I could arrange to move my items out, and Scott was extremely helpful on my last day there (extending my gate access hours by two hours to accommodate my needs). If I ever need a storage unit again, and am in this North County area, I‚Äôd definitely use StorQuest - Carlsbad / Campbell again!</review>< Pictures>

< Review>
They are the best.

Temperature control very good (best I've seen); very clean; very well lighted; good fire protection system and policies, a modern, multi-level security system, close access to all units; and the friendly staff is helpful and efficient with whatever you need (specialty boxes, bigger unit(s), etc.).  I looked at half a dozen local places -- they all looked fairly good -- before choosing StorQuest -- it looked better -- and will definitely use them again if the need arises.  And best of all: You can look up (if you're outside) and maybe see a P-51 Mustang or a B-17, (but usually a corporate jet) less than 500 feet above you (it's just south of the normal Palomar Airport landing path, kitty-corner to the end of the runway)!  (Admittedly, if your boxes of old books and grandma's heirloom furniture is truly priceless to you, then for perfect security I suppose being nearly right under the approach to the busiest single-runway airport in the country is not a feature.  But if it means that much to you, you really need a different level of security/storage anyway! :-))</Review>

< text>
This place is clean and well kept and it was unfair of me to give Scott a mediocre rating.  He does a good job and will go out on a limb for his tenants.  What I didn't know about StorQuest is they do automatic rate increases, like everybody else, in certain months of the year.  To avoid this rate increase, the tenant can opt to pay upfront for a long term lease (6 mos.) to lock in their rate.  I don't believe other storage facilities offer this.  Based upon this new information, I have revised my rating to a Five Star.  This is a nice facility where you're stuff is safe and protected.
It's too bad there aren't more storage facilities to provide competition hereby keeping the rates low. Us Baby Boomers like to hold onto our old stuff in case we need to sell it to make ends meet.</text>
